  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;name=' + shelf_name + '&amp;a=' + action + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('cbHrCTgJA+25Zoy1GBhncp98HIIUWuLBWhrY8kkV15gUZdTaytsXFzW++A5meYHA1ovfm12HpWswE91ghYAh3Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&amp;book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;refresh=true' + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('cjwke6z76WwJDeyfKh8GCbdxhQgTnvs8/sc+7Hf4Uo0X6BuoXin9loXVmCRUfuC7/oZGEVpDvJaUzjt+u22kyA==')})
  }

    <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/5194.Michael_Crichton">About Michael Crichton</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/5194.Michael_Crichton"><img alt="5194" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1359042651p2/5194.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer7869357254984982609">Michael Crichton (1942–2008) was one of the most successful novelists of his generation, admired for his meticulous scientific research and fast-paced narrative. He graduated summa cum laude and earned his MD from Harvard Medical School in 1969. His first novel, <a title="Odds On" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18078737.Odds_On">Odds On</a> (1966), was written under the pseudonym <a title="John Lange" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/12619.John_Lange">John Lange</a> and was followed by seven more Lange novels. He also wrote as <a title="Michael Douglas" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/85503.Michael_Douglas">Michael Douglas</a></span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText7869357254984982609">Michael Crichton (1942–2008) was one of the most successful novelists of his generation, admired for his meticulous scientific research and fast-paced narrative. He graduated summa cum laude and earned his MD from Harvard Medical School in 1969. His first novel, <a title="Odds On" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18078737.Odds_On">Odds On</a> (1966), was written under the pseudonym <a title="John Lange" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/12619.John_Lange">John Lange</a> and was followed by seven more Lange novels. He also wrote as <a title="Michael Douglas" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/85503.Michael_Douglas">Michael Douglas</a> and <a title="Jeffery Hudson" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/607284.Jeffery_Hudson">Jeffery Hudson</a>. His novel <a title="A Case of Need" href="https://www.goodreads.com/search/search?q=A%20Case%20of%20Need">A Case of Need</a> won the Edgar Award in 1969. Popular throughout the world, he has sold more than 200 million books. His novels have been translated into thirty-eight languages, and thirteen have been made into films.<br /><br />Michael Crichton passed away from lymphoma in 2008. He was 66 years old.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="7869357254984982609">...more</a>

    </div>
    <a href="/author/show/5194.Michael_Crichton" class="actionLink moreLink">More about Michael Crichton...</a>

He must have dealt with engineers at GM. “Emotionally, they’re all thirteen years old, stuck at the age just before boys stop playing with toys, because they’ve discovered girls. They’re all still playing with toys. They have poor social skills, dress badly—but they’re extremely intelligent and well trained, and they are very arrogant in their way. Outsiders are definitely not allowed to play.”</span>
